CREATE TABLE Customer (
   customer_id varchar(4) not null,
   first_name  varchar(25) not null,
   last_name   varchar(25) not null,
   gender      char(1),
   age         number(4),
   address     varchar(60),
   country     varchar(25),
primary key(customer_id),
constraint chk_gender check (UPPER(gender) in ('M','F'))
);

CREATE TABLE Customer_Contact (
   phone_number varchar(14),
   customer_id  varchar(4) not null,
primary key(phone_number),
foreign key(customer_id) references Customer(customer_id)  
);

CREATE TABLE Customer_Email (
   email       varchar(40),
   customer_id varchar(4) not null,
primary key(email),
foreign key(customer_id) references Customer(customer_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Employee(
   employee_id varchar(4) not null,
   emp_name    varchar(30) not null,
   emp_age     int,
   emp_gender  char(1),
   emp_address varchar(50),
   salary      number(6,2),
primary key(employee_id),
constraint chk_emp_gender check (UPPER(emp_gender) in ('M','F'))
);

CREATE TABLE Employee_Contact (
   employee_pn  varchar(14),
   employee_id  varchar(4) not null,
primary key(employee_pn),
foreign key(employee_id) references Employee(employee_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Service_Category (
   service_type  varchar(25) not null,
   service_price number(6,2),
primary key(service_type),
constraint chk_service_type check (UPPER(service_type) in ('ROOM SERVICE','CUSTOMER SERVICE','CAR RENTAL SERVICE','ROOM CLEANING SERVICE','CATERING SERVICE'))
);

CREATE TABLE Service (
   service_id   varchar(5) not null,
   service_type varchar(25) not null,
   quantity     int,
primary key(service_id),
foreign key(service_type) references Service_Category(service_type)
);

CREATE TABLE Request(
   request_id   varchar(3) not null,
   customer_id  varchar(4),
   service_id   varchar(5),
   request_date date,
primary key(request_id),
foreign key(customer_id) references Customer(customer_id),
foreign key(service_id) references Service(service_id)  
);

CREATE TABLE Room_Type (
   room_type  varchar(20) not null,
   room_size  varchar(10),
   bed_size   varchar(15),
   room_price number(6,2),
primary key(room_type),
constraint chk_room_type check (UPPER(room_type) in ('BASIC','DOUBLE','TRIPLE','QUAD','TWIN','SUITE')),
constraint chk_room_size check (UPPER(room_size) in ('SMALL','MEDIUM','LARGE')),
constraint chk_bed_size check (UPPER(bed_size) in ('SMALL','MEDIUM','LARGE'))
);

CREATE TABLE Room (
   room_id     varchar(4) not null,
   room_type   varchar(20) not null,
   floor_no    number(1),
   room_number varchar(3),
primary key(room_id),
foreign key(room_type) references Room_Type(room_type)
);

CREATE TABLE Facilities (
   facility_id   varchar(4) not null,
   facility_type varchar(30),
   facility_fees number(6,2),
primary key(facility_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Booking (
   booking_id      varchar(4) not null,
   room_id     varchar(4) not null,
   facility_id   varchar(4) not null,
   arrival_date    date,
   departure_date  date,
   cust_quantity   number(2),
   customer_id     varchar(4) not null,
primary key(booking_id),
foreign key(customer_id) references Customer(customer_id),
foreign key(room_id) references Room(room_id),
foreign key(facility_id) references Facilities(facility_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Bill (
   bill_id      varchar(4) not null,
   booking_id   varchar(4) not null,
   SST          number(6,2),
   total_amount number(7,2),
   employee_id  varchar(4) not null,
primary key(bill_id),
foreign key(booking_id) references Booking(booking_id),
foreign key(employee_id) references Employee(employee_id)
);
